--
-- Cấu trúc bảng cho bảng `hanghoa_binhluan`
--

CREATE TABLE `hanghoa_binhluan` (
  `Id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `MaHang` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `ParentId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `TenNguoiDung` varchar(120) NOT NULL,
  `NoiDung` text NOT NULL,
  `HinhAnh` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `SoSao` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT 5,
  `NguoiDungId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `VaiTroNguoiDung` varchar(30) DEFAULT NULL,
  `NgayTao` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

--
-- Đang đổ dữ liệu cho bảng `hanghoa_binhluan`
--

INSERT INTO `hanghoa_binhluan` (`Id`, `MaHang`, `ParentId`, `TenNguoiDung`, `NoiDung`, `HinhAnh`, `SoSao`, `NguoiDungId`, `VaiTroNguoiDung`, `NgayTao`) VALUES

(5, 'HH241', 4, 'kiet', 'cvvcv', NULL, 0, 5, 'khachhang', '2026-04-12 03:58:58');

--
-- Cấu trúc bảng cho bảng `users`
--

CREATE TABLE `users` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(150) NOT NULL,
  `password` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `provider` enum('local','google','facebook','github') DEFAULT 'local',
  `avatar` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` enum('active','inactive') DEFAULT 'active',
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp(),
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp() ON UPDATE current_timestamp(),
  `role` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'khachhang',
  `admin_created` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

--
-- Cấu trúc cho view `vw_product_detail_page`
--
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS `vw_product_detail_page`;

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW `vw_product_detail_page` AS SELECT `h`.`MaHang` AS `id`, `h`.`TenHang` AS `name`, `h`.`DVT` AS `unit`, `h`.`DonGia` AS `price_before_tax`, `h`.`SoTienCoThue` AS `price`, `h`.`VAT` AS `vat`, `h`.`HinhAnh` AS `image`, `nh`.`MaNhomHang` AS `group_code`, `nh`.`TenNhomHang` AS `group_name`, coalesce(`m`.`MoTaChiTiet`,'') AS `detail_description` FROM ((`hanghoa` `h` left join `nhomhang` `nh` on(`nh`.`MaNhomHang` = `h`.`MaNhomHang`)) left join `hanghoa_mota_chitiet` `m` on(`m`.`MaHang` = `h`.`MaHang`)) ;

--
-- Chỉ mục cho các bảng đã đổ
--

-- Chỉ mục cho bảng `chitietphieuxuat`
--
ALTER TABLE `chitietphieuxuat`
  ADD PRIMARY KEY (`IdPhieuXuat`,`MaHang`),
  ADD KEY `MaHang` (`MaHang`);

ALTER TABLE `chucvu`
  ADD PRIMARY KEY (`MaCV`);
